This reviewer was not provided any incentive by G2 for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: In-app</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-6"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2023-12-11" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2023-12-11">Dec 11, 2023</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/impact-com-performance/reviews/impact-com-performance-review-8993006"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Great for tracking, optimize is debatable though"</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The ease of setting up partners and providing them with trackable links and assets, the marketplace, and the day to day support I get from my success rep. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about impact.com/performance?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">- Adding a new event has proven more difficult than it should and we're still not sure why it's not working. 
</p><p class="formatted-text">
</p><p class="formatted-text">- Optimize leaves a lot to be desired in clearly showing the customer journey and how the affiliate channel enhances performance across other channels such as influencer, and SEM - the report is really not easily digestible. Further, learning how to build custom charts has been a pain point and no one rep can seem to give me a meaningful toutorial or intruction on how to build my own or,  best leverage/decipher the pre-populated charts within optimize. This along with benchmarking for a niche brand are some areas that I feel need more attention. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-8993006 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is impact.com/performance solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partner management and attribution are great, I'm able to quickly onboard and equip partners and manage their actions day to day. I'm not solving for customer journey analytics yet (see optimize feedback) and would like to better connect with publishers and affilaites via the marketplace but find that to be hit or miss. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized"
